Ka hun a tung nai kei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">A nu in nasemte kiangah, “Ama hong cih bangbang in na hih un,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Tualai ah Judah mite kisiansuahna a kizang, khat sungah tui gallon 20 gallon 30 bang a ta thei, thambel guk a om hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Hih bel teng tui dim un,” a ci hi. Tua ciangin amaute in belgong dong dimin tui a sung uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Zeisu in, “Tu in, pawlkhat suak unla, pawi ukpa va pia un,” a ci hi. Amaute in zong suakin a pia uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Pawi ukpa in lenggahzu a kisuaksak tua tui a ciam hi. Tua ciangin a nungzuite in amah a um uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Tua khit ciangin Zeisu in a nu, a sanggamte le a nungzuite tawh Capernaum khua ah paisuk uh a, tualai ah tawmvei sung a taam uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tu in Judah mite Paisan Pawi hong naita ahih manin Jerusalem khuapi ah Zeisu a paito hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Biakinnpi huang sungah bawng zuak, tuu zuak, vakhu zuakte le sumkhek in summet bawla a omte a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Amah in khautep khat bawl in tuute, bawngte le mi khempeuh biakinnpi huang sung panin a hawlkhia hi. Sumkhekteɠ sumteng buakkhiatsak in sabuaite zong a lumlet hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Vakhu zuakte kiangah, “Hihte lakhia un! Amah a kipan a tate le a ganhingte in hih tuikhuk tui a nek uh ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Zeisu in tua nu kiangah, “Hih tui a dawn mi peuhmah a dangtakkik ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Ahih hangin ken ka piak tui a dawn mi peuhmah in a dangtak ngei nawn kei ding hi. Tua khit ciangin hong paikik un,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Numei in, “Pasal ka nei kei hi,” a cih ciangin, Zeisu in, “ ‘Pasal ka nei kei hi,’ na cih pen a maan hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Banghang hiam cihleh pasal nga na nei khinzo a, tu‑a na neih pen zong na pasal hilo ahih manin thuman na gen hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Numei in, “Sia aw, kamsang khat na hih lam kong thei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Ka pute ka pate un hih mualtung ah Pasian a bia uh hi. No Judah mite in Jerusalem khuapi bekah Pasian kibia ding hi na ci uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Zeisu in, “Numei aw, ka thu gen hong um in. Hih mualtung ah ahi a, Jerusalem khuapi ah ahi zongin Pa a kibiakloh hun hong tung ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Note in na theih lohpi uh na bia uh hi. Kote in ka theih uh ka bia uh hi. Banghang hiam cihleh Judah mite tung panin hotkhiatna hong piang hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Ahih hangin a bia taktakte in kha le thuman thutak tawh Pasian a biak ding hun uh tu in hong tung zota hi. Banghang hiam cihleh tua banga amah a bia ding mite Pa in a zong hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Pasian in Kha ahi hi. Amah a biate in lungsim le thuman thutak tawh a bia ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Numei in ama kiangah, “Khazih kici Messiah hong pai ding hi cih ka thei hi. Amah a hong tun ciangin na khempeuh a hong hilhcian ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Zeisu in, “Nangmah tawh a kiho keimah in tua Messiah ka hi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Tua laitak in a nungzuite hong tungkik uh a, tua numei tawh a kihona lamdang a sa uh hi. Ahi zongin, “Bang na deihna ahi hiam?” cih ahi a, “Banghang in tua nu hopih na hi hiam?” cih ahi zongin kuamah in a dong ngam kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Tua khit ciangin numei in a tuibel nusia in khua sungah tai a, a khuapihte kiangah,</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">“Hong pai unla, ka gamtatna khempeuh hong genpa hong en un. Midangte in na kho uh a, note in amaute sepsa a la ding na hi uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"39\"><sup data-verseid=\"39\">&nbsp;<!-- -->39<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"39\">“Ka gamtatna khempeuh hong gen hi,” a ci tua numeinu teci panna hangin Samaria khua mi tampi in Zeisu a um uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"40\"><sup data-verseid=\"40\">&nbsp;<!-- -->40<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"40\">Samaria khua mite Zeisu kianga tun uh ciangin amau khua ah a taam dingin kho uh a, tua khua ah ni nih a taam hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"41\"><sup data-verseid=\"41\">&nbsp;<!-- -->41<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"41\">Ama thugenna hangin thu‑um mi tampi a kibehlap hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"42\"><sup data-verseid=\"42\">&nbsp;<!-- -->42<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"42\">Tua khit ciangin amaute in numeinu kiangah, “Nang nong gen hang beka um ka hi nawn kei uh hi. Hong pai inla, hong damsak in,” ci in a thum hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"48\"><sup data-verseid=\"48\">&nbsp;<!-- -->48<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"48\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Note in limlamdangte le nalamdang lianpite na muh kei ngal uh leh na um peuhmah kei ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"49\"><sup data-verseid=\"49\">&nbsp;<!-- -->49<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"49\">Ulianpa in, “Sia aw, ka tapa a sihma in hong paisuk tapeuh in!” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"50\"><sup data-verseid=\"50\">&nbsp;<!-- -->50<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"50\">Zeisu in, “Ciah in na tapa a damzo hi,” a ci hi. Keima kiang hong zuan mi nitawp ni ciangin ka thokiksak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"45\"><sup data-verseid=\"45\">&nbsp;<!-- -->45<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"45\">Kamsangte laibu sunga a kigelh mah bangin, ‘Pasian in amaute khempeuh thu hilh ding hi.’ Tua hi a, Pa thu za a, a thei mi khempeuh in keima kiang hong zuan uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"46\"><sup data-verseid=\"46\">&nbsp;<!-- -->46<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"46\">Pasian kiang pana hong paipa longal kuamah in Pa a mu ngei kei hi. Tua pa bekin Pa a mu khinzo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"47\"><sup data-verseid=\"47\">&nbsp;<!-- -->47<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"47\">Aman takpi kong cih in ah, kei hong um mi in nuntak tawntungna a neizo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"48\"><sup data-verseid=\"48\">&nbsp;<!-- -->48<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"48\">Keimah in nuntakna anlum ka hi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"49\"><sup data-verseid=\"49\">&nbsp;<!-- -->49<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"49\">Na pute na pate un gamlak ah manna a nek uh hangin a si veve uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"50\"><sup data-verseid=\"50\">&nbsp;<!-- -->50<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"50\">Vantung panin a hong pai hih anlum a ne mi a si kei ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"51\"><sup data-verseid=\"51\">&nbsp;<!-- -->51<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"51\">Keimah in vantung panin hong pai nuntakna anlum ka hi hi. Leitung mite nuntak nadingin ka piak ding anlum in hih ka pumpi ahi hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"52\"><sup data-verseid=\"52\">&nbsp;<!-- -->52<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"52\">Tua ciangin Judah mite in, “Hihpa in eite nek dingin ama pumpi hong bangci piak theih ding ahi hiam?” ci in a kinial uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"53\"><sup data-verseid=\"53\">&nbsp;<!-- -->53<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"53\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in, “Aman takpi kong cih in ah, Mihing Tapa pumpi ne a, a si na dawn kei uh leh nuntakna na ngah kei ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"54\"><sup data-verseid=\"54\">&nbsp;<!-- -->54<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"54\">Ka pumpi ne a, ka si a dawn mi kuama peuh in nuntak tawntungna a nei hi. Nitawp ni ciangin tua mi ka thokiksak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"55\"><sup data-verseid=\"55\">&nbsp;<!-- -->55<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"55\">Banghang hiam cihleh ka pumpi in an taktak hi a, ka si in dawn ding taktak ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"56\"><sup data-verseid=\"56\">&nbsp;<!-- -->56<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"56\">Ka pumpi ne a, ka si a dawn mi in keima sungah teeng a, ama sungah kei ka teeng hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"57\"><sup data-verseid=\"57\">&nbsp;<!-- -->57<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"57\">A nungta ka Pa in kei hong sawl a, Pa hanga ka nuntak mah bangin keima sa a ne mi in keima hangin a nungta ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"58\"><sup data-verseid=\"58\">&nbsp;<!-- -->58<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"58\">Hih anlum in vantung pana hong paisuk ahi hi. Na pu na pate un manna ne a, a sih veve uh bang hilo in hih anlum a ne mi a nungta tawntung ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"59\"><sup data-verseid=\"59\">&nbsp;<!-- -->59<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"59\">Hih thute Capernaum khua kikhopna inn sunga a hilh ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"60\"><sup data-verseid=\"60\">&nbsp;<!-- -->60<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"60\">Tua hi a, a nungzui tampite in tua thuhilhna a zak uh ciangin, “Hih thu in thuhaksa ahi hi. Kua in theitel zo ding ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"61\"><sup data-verseid=\"61\">&nbsp;<!-- -->61<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"61\">Nungzuite in hih thu hangin a phunna Zeisu in a theih ciangin amaute kiangah, “Hih thu in note hong lungkiasak ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"62\"><sup data-verseid=\"62\">&nbsp;<!-- -->62<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"62\">Tua ahih leh Mihing Tapa a masa a a omna munah a kahto mu le uh teh bangci ding na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"63\"><sup data-verseid=\"63\">&nbsp;<!-- -->63<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"63\">Kha in nuntakna pia a, ci le sa in phattuamna bangmah a pia kei hi. Nangmah in nuntak tawntungna thu na nei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"69\"><sup data-verseid=\"69\">&nbsp;<!-- -->69<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"69\">A nungta Pasian Tapa Khazih na hih lam kote in thei in kong um uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"70\"><sup data-verseid=\"70\">&nbsp;<!-- -->70<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"70\">Zeisu in, “No sawm le nihte keima kong teel hi a, note sung panin khatin dawi hilo ahi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"71\"><sup data-verseid=\"71\">&nbsp;<!-- -->71<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"71\">Tua bang a cih ciangin sawm le nihte lakah amah a lehhek ding Simon tapa Judas Iscariot a cihna ahi hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp;     "7": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">7</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Hih thuteng khit ciangin Galilee gam sungah Zeisu a zin kawikawi hi. Banghang hiam cihleh Judah mite in amah thahsawm uh ahih manin Judea gam sungah a zin nuam kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Tu in Judah mite Buuk Pawi hong naita hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua ahih ciangin a sanggamte in ama kiangah, “Na nungzuite in zong na bawl na nasepte a muh theih nadingun hih mun pan paikhia inla, Judea gamah va pai in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Mite theih ding a ut mite in a simtham in na sem lo uh hi. Greek mite laka a kithehthang i mipihte kiangah pai in, Greek mite thu va hilh sawm ahi hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"36\"><sup data-verseid=\"36\">&nbsp;<!-- -->36<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"36\">‘Nong zong ding uh a, nong mu kei ding uh hi.     "8": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">8</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Zeisu ahih leh Tanluan mualtung ah a kahto hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Zingsang phalvak tungin biakinnpi huang sungah Zeisu a paikik hi. Ahi zongin nang bang na ci ngaihsut hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Hih bangin a dot uh pen Zeisu mawhmat nuama a ze‑et uh ahi hi. Thuman thutak gen napi banghang in hong um lo na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"47\"><sup data-verseid=\"47\">&nbsp;<!-- -->47<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"47\">Pasian tawh a kipawlte in Pasian thugente a zathei hi. Pasian tawh kipawl lo na hih manun Pasian thugente na zathei kei uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"48\"><sup data-verseid=\"48\">&nbsp;<!-- -->48<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"48\">Tua ciangin Judah mite in ama kiangah, “Nang Samaria mi, dawilawm nei kong cih uh a maan mah hilo ahi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"49\"><sup data-verseid=\"49\">&nbsp;<!-- -->49<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"49\">Zeisu in, “Dawilawm nei ka hi kei a, ka Pa a pahtawi ka hi hi. Ahih hangin note in kei nong pahtawi kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"50\"><sup data-verseid=\"50\">&nbsp;<!-- -->50<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"50\">Ka minthan nading ka zong kei hi. Ka minthan nading a zong khat om a, amah in thu zong a khen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"51\"><sup data-verseid=\"51\">&nbsp;<!-- -->51<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"51\">Aman takpi kong cih in ah, mi khatpeuh in ka thugente a zuih leh a si ngei kei ding hi,” ci in a dawng hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"52\"><sup data-verseid=\"52\">&nbsp;<!-- -->52<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"52\">Tua ciangin Judah mite in ama kiangah, “Tu in, dawilawm nei na hih lam kong theitel taktak uh hi! Abraham le kamsangte zong si khinzo napi, ‘Mi khatpeuh in ka thu a zuih leh a si ngei kei ding hi,’ na ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"53\"><sup data-verseid=\"53\">&nbsp;<!-- -->53<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"53\">A sisa ka pa uh Abraham sangin lianzaw na hi hiam? Kamsang khempeuh zong a si khinzo uh hi. Nang bang mi kisa na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"54\"><sup data-verseid=\"54\">&nbsp;<!-- -->54<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"54\">Zeisu in, “Kei le kei a kipahtawi hi leng tua kipahtawina in khiatna neilo hi. Kei hong pahtawipa in ka Pa hi a, kote Pasian hi na cihpa uh ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"55\"><sup data-verseid=\"55\">&nbsp;<!-- -->55<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"55\">Ahih hangin note in amah na thei kei uh hi. Ken ka hih leh ka thei hi. Amah ka thei kei hi cileng, note mah banga zuaugen ka hi ding hi. Ken amah ka thei a, ama thugente ka zui hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"56\"><sup data-verseid=\"56\">&nbsp;<!-- -->56<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"56\">Na pa uh Abraham in ka ni a muh ding lawp mahmah a, a muh ciangin zong a lungdam mahmah hi,” ci in a dawng hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"57\"><sup data-verseid=\"57\">&nbsp;<!-- -->57<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"57\">Tua ciangin Judah mite in, “Nang kum 50 zong pha nailo napi in Abraham mu ngei na hi hiam?” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"58\"><sup data-verseid=\"58\">&nbsp;<!-- -->58<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"58\">Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Aman takpi kong cih in ah, Abraham a om ma in KEI KA OM HI,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"59\"><sup data-verseid=\"59\">&nbsp;<!-- -->59<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"59\">Tua ciangin amaute in amah a den nadingin suang a tawm uh hi. Ahih hangin Zeisu in amaute lak nawkin biakinnpi huang sung panin a gelkhia hi.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>",
    "9": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">9</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua bangin Zeisu a paikhiat laitak in mittawsa a suak mi khat a mu hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">A nungzuite in, “Rabbi aw, kua mawhna hanga hihpa mittawsa in suak ahi hiam? (Siloam a khiatna in, Kisawl hi, cihna ahi hi.)     "10": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">10</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Zeisu in, “Aman takpi kong cih in ah, tuukhumna kongpi tawn loin mundang pan kahto a a lut mi in guta le misuam ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Ahi zongin kongpi tawna a lut mi in tuucingpa ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Kong cingpa in amah kong hon a, tuute in ama aw a thei uh hi. Amah in a tuute a minin samin a pusuahpih hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Amah in a tuute khahkhia in amaute mai ah amah pai a, tuute in ama aw thei uh ahih manin a nung a zui uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Midang mawkmawk khat a pai hangin tua pa aw thei lo uh ahih manin zui loin a taisan ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Zeisu in hih thugentehna tawh thu a gen hangin amaute in bang thu gen hiam cih a thei zo kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Tua ahih manin Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Aman takpi kong cih in ah, keimah in tuute aa dingin kongpi ka hi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Ka mai‑a hong paite khempeuh, guta le misuam ahih manun tuute in amaute aw a thei kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Keimah in kongpi ka hi hi. Kei hong tawna a lut mi peuhmah khamuang dinga, sungtum pusuak in lonona mun a mu ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"10\"><sup data-verseid=\"10\">&nbsp;<!-- -->10<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"10\">Gutapa in a gu ding, a that ding le a susia ding bekin a hong pai hi.     "14": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">14</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Zeisu in, “Note na lungkham kei un. Pasian um unla, kei zong hong um un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Ka Pa inn sungah om nading mun tampi a om hi. Note om nading mun bawlkhol dingin ka va pai ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Va pai in note aa ding mun ka bawl khit ciangin kong paikik dinga ka omna munah note zong na om theih nadingun ka kiangah kong la ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Ka pai nading mun na thei uh a, a lampi zong na thei uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Thomas in ama kiangah, “Topa aw, na pai nading mun theilo ka hih manun a lampi bangci theih ding ka hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Keimah in lampi, thuman thutak le nuntakna ka hi hi. Kei tungtawn loin kuamah in Pa kiang a tung thei kei ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"7\"><sup data-verseid=\"7\">&nbsp;<!-- -->7<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"7\">Kei nong theih khit uh leh ka Pa zong na theikhin ding uh hi. Tu a kipan amah na thei uh a, na mu zo uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"8\"><sup data-verseid=\"8\">&nbsp;<!-- -->8<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"8\">Philip in ama kiangah, “Topa aw, Pa hong lak lecin ka lungkim ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"9\"><sup data-verseid=\"9\">&nbsp;<!-- -->9<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"9\">Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Philip aw, note tawh hih tanvei hong omkhawm khinzo napi ing in kei hong thei lo lailai na hi hiam? Note kianga kong gen thute keima ut thu a kong gentawm hilo in ka sunga a teeng ka Pa in na a sem ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Pa sungah kei ka om a, kei sungah Pa a om hi ka cih thu hong um in. Ahih keileh zong ka bawl nate hangin hong um in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Aman takpi kong cih in ah, kei hong um mi in keima nasep teng mah a sem ding hi. Ka Pa kiangah ciah ding ka hih manin, keima septe sanga a lianzaw zong a sem ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Keima min suanga na nget khempeuh uh Tapa tungtawn in Pa min a than theih nadingin kong pia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Keima min suanga na khat peuhpeuh na nget uh leh kong pia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">“Kei nong it uh leh kong thupiakte na zui un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Ka Pa kiangah ka ngen dinga, amah in note tawh hong omkhawm tawntung dingin a dang Huhpa khat hong pia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Tua Huhpa in thuman thutak Kha ahi hi. Leitung mite in amah mu lo in thei lo uh ahih manin a sang thei kei ding uh hi. Ahi zongin amah in note tawh hong teengkhawm in note sungah hong om ding ahih manin amah na thei ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Tagah bangin note kong nusia kei dinga, note kiangah kong paikik ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Tawmvei khit ciangin leitung mite in a hong mu nawn kei ding uh hi. Ahi zongin note in nong mu ding uh hi. Banghang hiam cihleh kei ka nuntak manin note zong na nungta ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Pa sungah kei ka om a, kei sungah note om in note sungah zong kei ka om lam tua ni ciangin na thei ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Keima thupiakte nei a, a zui mi peuhmah in kei hong it mi ahi hi. Kei hong it mi ka Pa in zong it dinga, ken zong amah it in ama tungah ka kilang ding hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Iscariot a hilo Judas dang khatpen in ama kiangah, “Topa aw, leitung mite tungah kilang loin kote tung bekah hong kilang ning na cih koici bang thu ahi hiam?” ci in a dong hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Zeisu in dawngkik in, “Mi khatpeuh in kei a hong it leh ka thu a zui ding hi. Na zak uh ka thugente keima thu hilo in kei hong sawlpa ka Pa thu ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">“Note tawh kong omkhop sungin hih thute kong genzo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Ahi zongin Pa in kei minin a hong sawl ding Huhpa Kha Siangtho in thu khempeuh hong hilh dinga note kianga kong gensa thu khempeuh a hong phawkkiksak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Lungmuanna kong nusiat hi. Keima lungmuanna note kong pia a, leitung hong piak bangin ka hong pia kei hi. Lungkham kei unla, lau kei un.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">“‘Ka va ciah dinga, note kiangah kong paikik ding hi,’ kong cihna thu na zazo uh hi.     "15": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">15</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Zeisu in, “Keimah in lenggui maan taktak ka hi a, ka Pa in lenggui lo neipa ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Kei tungah om napi a gahlo hiang khempeuh amah in sattan dinga, a gah hiang khempeuh a gah semsem nadingin a heuhsiang ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Note tunga kong gensa thu hangin tu in na siangta uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Kei sungah om tawntung un.     "16": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">16</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">“Note na puk loh nadingun hih thute kong genzo hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Kikhopna inn panin note hong hawlkhia ding uh hi. Hi hi, note hong that mi khatpeuh in Pasian nasem in a kingaihsut uh hun hong tung ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Amaute in Pa thei lo uh a, kei zong hong thei lo uh ahih manin tua bangin hong gamta ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Tua mite thu hong gen khinzo ka hih manin a hun hong tun ciangin na phawkkik theih nadingun hih thute kong gen hi. A zaksa thute bek hong gen dinga, hong pianglai ding thute zong hong hilh ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Amah in kei tung pana a ngah thute note tungah hong pulak ding ahih manin ka min a thangsak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Ka Pa neihsa khempeuh kei aa ahi hi. Tua ahih manin kei tung pana a ngah thute note tungah hong pulak ding hi ci a, hong gen ka hi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">“Pa kiangah pai ding ka hih manin tawlkhat sung nong mu kei ding uh a, tawlkhat khit ciangin nong mukik ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"17\"><sup data-verseid=\"17\">&nbsp;<!-- -->17<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"17\">Tua ciangin a nungzuite pawlkhat in, “ ‘Pa kiangah ka pai ding hi,’ a cih pen le, ‘Tawlkhat sung nong mu kei ding uh a, tawlkhat khit ciangin nong mukik ding uh hi,’ a cih pen in bang a cihnopna hi ding ahi hiam?” a kici uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Tua ahih manin amaute in, “ ‘Tawlkhat sung’ a cih pen bang a cihnopna hi peuhmah ding ahi hiam? A thugen i thei zo peuhmah kei hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Amaute in thu khat dongnuam uh hi cih Zeisu in a theih ciangin amaute kiangah, “ ‘Tawlkhat sung nong mu kei ding uh a, tawlkhat khit ciangin nong mukik ding uh hi,’ kong cih bang ka cihnopna hiam ci in khat le khat a kidong hingel uh teh maw?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Aman takpi kong cih in ah, note kapin na tamlo ding uh a, leitung mite ahih leh a nuam ding uh hi. Na dah uh hangin na dahna teng uh nuamna hong suak ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Numei khat nau a suah ding ciangin lau‑a a dah hangin nau a suah khit phetin leitung ah mihing khat hong piang ahih manin lungdam in a Nausuah gimna khempeuh a phawk nawn kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Tuamah bangin tu in na dah mahmah uh hangin kong mukik dinga, tua hun ciangin na lungdam ding uh hi. Tua na lungdamna uh kuamah in hong sutkhia thei kei ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Tua ni ciangin bangmah nong ngen nawn kei ding uh hi. Aman takpi kong cih in ah, keima min tawh Pa kianga na nget peuhpeuh uh amah in hong pia ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Tu dongin keima minin bangmah na ngen nai kei uh hi. Ngen un. Na lungdamna uh a kicin nadingin na ngah ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">“Hih thute note kiangah gentehna tawh kong gen hi. Ahih hangin gentehna tawh hong gen nawnlo in Pa thu a teltak a kong gen ding hun hong tung ding hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Tua ni ciangin keima min suangin thu na ngen ding uh hi. Note aa dingin Pa kiangah thu kong ngetsak ding hi a ci ka hi kei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Banghang hiam cihleh note in kei hong it in, Pasian kiang panin hong pai hi ci in hong um na hih manun, Pa mahmah in zong note hong it hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"28\"><sup data-verseid=\"28\">&nbsp;<!-- -->28<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"28\">Pa kiang panin leitung ah kong pai a, leitung nusia in Pa kiangah ka ciahkik ding hi,” ci in Zeisu in a gen hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"29\"><sup data-verseid=\"29\">&nbsp;<!-- -->29<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"29\">A nungzuite in ama kiangah, “En in, tu in gentehna zang loin kiteltak in thu nong genta hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"30\"><sup data-verseid=\"30\">&nbsp;<!-- -->30<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"30\">Na khempeuh na thei a, kuamah in thu hong sittel ding kul lo hi cih ka theita uh hi. Hih thu hang mahin Pasian kiang pana hong pai na hi hi ci in kong um uh hi,” a ci uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"31\"><sup data-verseid=\"31\">&nbsp;<!-- -->31<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"31\">Zeisu in amaute kiangah, “Tu in hong um takpi na hi uh hiam?</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">En un, na inn ciat uh zuanin kithehthang a kei guak nong nusiat ding uh hun hong tung ding pen tu in hong tungzo hi. Ahih hangin kei guak ka om kei a, Pa in hong ompih hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">“Keima sungah lungmuanna na neih theih nadingun hih thute kong genzo hi.     "17": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">17</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Zeisu in hih thute a gen khit ciangin vantung lam ento a, “Pa aw, a hun hong tungzo hi.     "18": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">18</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Zeisu in hih bangin thu a nget khit ciangin a nungzuite tawh paikhia a, Kidron lui gal khat a om huan khat sungah a lut uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Zeisu le a nungzuite tua munah paikhawm zel uh ahih manin amah a lehhekpa Judas in zong tua mun a thei hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua ciangin Judas in galkap honkhatɠ, siampi liante le Pharisee pawlte kiang pana kisawl biakinn cingte pawlkhat hong makaih in huan sungah a hong pai uh hi. Amaute in meivak, meilah le hiamte a tawi uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Zeisu in ama tunga piang ding teng thei ahih manin amaute kiangah va pai a, “Kua zong na hi uh hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Amaute in, “Nazareth khua mi Zeisu,” a ci uh hi. Tua nasempa min in Malchus ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"11\"><sup data-verseid=\"11\">&nbsp;<!-- -->11<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"11\">Zeisu in Peter kiangah, “Na namsau a paai ah siatkik in. Ka Pa in hong piak hai dawn loin om ding ka hi hiam?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"12\"><sup data-verseid=\"12\">&nbsp;<!-- -->12<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"12\">Tua khit ciangin galkaphonɠ a kipan galkap mangpaɠ le biakinn cing Judah mite in Zeisu manin a hen uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"13\"><sup data-verseid=\"13\">&nbsp;<!-- -->13<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"13\">Tua khit ciangin tua kuma Siampi Ukpa Caiaphas sunghpa Annas kiangah a paipih masa uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"14\"><sup data-verseid=\"14\">&nbsp;<!-- -->14<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"14\">Tu in Caiaphas in mipi tangin mi khat a sih ding hoih zaw hi ci in Judah mite thu a hilhpa ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"15\"><sup data-verseid=\"15\">&nbsp;<!-- -->15<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"15\">Tu in Simon Peter le a dang nungzuite khatin Zeisu a zui uh hi. Tua nungzuipa pen Siampi Ukpa tawh kimeltheih ahih manin, Siampi Ukpa inntual ah Zeisu tawh a lutkhawm uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"16\"><sup data-verseid=\"16\">&nbsp;<!-- -->16<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"16\">Peter ahih leh kongpi pualam ah dingin a om hi. Peter in, “Ka hi kei hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Tu in khuadam ahih manin, tua muna ding nasemte le biakinn cingte in meihol cih in a awi uh hi. Peter zong tua mite tawh dingkhawm in mei a awi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Tu in Siampi Ukpa in Zeisu kiangah a nungzuite thu le a thuhilhna tawh kisai thute a dong hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Leitung mite tungah a kilang in thu ka genzo hi.     "19": "<main class=\"\"><div class=\"chapter justify\"><span class=\"drop-caps\">19</span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"1\"><sup data-verseid=\"1\">&nbsp;<!-- -->1<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"1\">Tua khit ciangin Pilate in ama kiangah Zeisu samin a satsak hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"2\"><sup data-verseid=\"2\">&nbsp;<!-- -->2<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"2\">Galkapte in linglukhu bawl in khusak uh a, puan dupsan khat a silhsak uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"3\"><sup data-verseid=\"3\">&nbsp;<!-- -->3<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"3\">Tua khit ciangin, “Dam maw, Judah mite Kumpipa!” ci in a beng uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"4\"><sup data-verseid=\"4\">&nbsp;<!-- -->4<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"4\">Pilate zong khatvei paikhiakik in amaute kiangah, “En un, hihpa tungah khialhna ka muh loh lam na theih nadingun note kiangah kong puakkik hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"5\"><sup data-verseid=\"5\">&nbsp;<!-- -->5<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"5\">Tua ciangin Zeisu in ling lukhu khusa le puan dupsan silhsa in a hong paikhia hi. Pilate in amaute kiangah, “Hih mipa en un!” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"6\"><sup data-verseid=\"6\">&nbsp;<!-- -->6<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"6\">Tua ciangin siampi liante le biakinn cingte in amah mu uh a, “Khailum in, khailum in!” ci in a kiko uh hi. Tua pen Lai Siangtho sung a, “Amaute in ka puan hawm uh a, Ka puanak a ngah nadingun, Lai‑ai a san uh hi,” ci a, a kigelhsa thu a tangtun nadingin galkapte in hi bangin ahih uh ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Tu in Zeisu a kikhaina singlamteh kiangah a nu, a nu sanggamnu ahi Clopas zi Mary le Magdala khua mi Mary‑te a ding uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"26\"><sup data-verseid=\"26\">&nbsp;<!-- -->26<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"26\">Tua bangin Zeisu in a nu le ama it nungzuipa a muh ciangin a nu kiangah, “Numei aw, na tapa en in!” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"27\"><sup data-verseid=\"27\">&nbsp;<!-- -->27<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"27\">Tua khit ciangin a nungzuipa kiangah, “Na nu en in!” a ci hi. Sabbath ni in singlamteh tungah misi luangte kikoih theilo ahih manin a khete uh kikuaitan in misi luangte a kilakkhiat nadingin Judah mite in Pilate kiangah a ngen uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"32\"><sup data-verseid=\"32\">&nbsp;<!-- -->32<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"32\">Tua ciangin class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"33\"><sup data-verseid=\"33\">&nbsp;<!-- -->33<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"33\">Ahih hangin Zeisu kiang a tun uh ciangin amah na si khinzo ahih manin a khe a sutan nawn kei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"34\"><sup data-verseid=\"34\">&nbsp;<!-- -->34<!-- Zeisu in, “Ka tuute na vak in.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"18\"><sup data-verseid=\"18\">&nbsp;<!-- -->18<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"18\">Aman takpi kong cih in ah, na khangno lai in na kawng gakin na utna peuhpeuh ah na pai hi. Ahih hangin na upat ciangin na khut na zan dinga, midangte in na kawng hong hensak in na pai nop lohna munah hong paipih ding uh hi,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"19\"><sup data-verseid=\"19\">&nbsp;<!-- -->19<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"19\">Hih thu in, Peter in ama sihzia tawh Pasian minthangsak ding cih a gennopna ahi hi. Tua khit ciangin Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Hong zui in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"20\"><sup data-verseid=\"20\">&nbsp;<!-- -->20<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"20\">Tua ciangin Peter a kihei leh ama nungah Zeisu in a it nungzuipa in a zuih lam a mu hi. Tua pa pen nitak an a neklai un Zeisu ang ah a kingap kawmsa a, “Topa aw, nang hong lehhek ding kua pen ahi hiam?” ci in a dong pa ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"21\"><sup data-verseid=\"21\">&nbsp;<!-- -->21<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"21\">Peter in tua pa a muh ciangin Zeisu kiangah, “Topa aw, hihpa e leh, bangci ding a hia?” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"22\"><sup data-verseid=\"22\">&nbsp;<!-- -->22<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"22\">Zeisu in ama kiangah, “Kong paikik dong hihpa ka nuntak suaksak nop leh bang phamawh sa na hi hiam? Nang na hih leh ka nung hong zui in,” a ci hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"23\"><sup data-verseid=\"23\">&nbsp;<!-- -->23<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"23\">Hih thu hangin tua nungzuipa si lo ding hi ci in nungzuite lakah a thang hi. Ahih hangin Zeisu in amah si lo ding hi a ci hilo a, “Kong paikik dong amah ka nuntak suaksak nop leh bang phamawh sa na hi hiam?” a ci bek ahi hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"24\"><sup data-verseid=\"24\">&nbsp;<!-- -->24<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"24\">Hih thu khempeuh teci panga a gelhpa in tua nungzuipa ahi hi. Ama teci panna a maan hi cih kote in ka thei uh hi.</span></span><span style=\"background:linear-gradient(inherit,inherit)\" class=\"align-left\" data-verseid=\"25\"><sup data-verseid=\"25\">&nbsp;<!-- -->25<!-- -->&nbsp;</sup><span data-verseid=\"25\">Zeisu in a bawl nalamdang tampi zong a omlai hi. Tuate a bantak in kigelh leh a kigelhna laibute leitung ah ta zo in ka um kei hi. Amen.</span></span></div><section class=\"information\"><button class=\"information-toggle\" type=\"button\">Copyrighted Material<!-- -->&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class=\"learn-more\">Learn More</span><svg class=\"icon\"><use xmlns:xlink=\"http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink\" xlink:href=\"/svglist.svg#arrow_down\"></use></svg></button><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"rah-static rah-static--height-zero \" style=\"height:0;overflow:hidden\"><div><div style=\"max-height:0\" class=\"copyrights-section\"><div class=\"ot-copyright\"></div><div class=\"nt-copyright\"></div></div></div></div><div class=\"ministry-statement\"><div class=\"ministry-tagline\">©<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.bible.is\">Bible.is</a>, a ministry of<!-- -->&nbsp;<a rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.faithcomesbyhearing.com\">Faith Comes By Hearing</a>&nbsp;<!-- -->®.<!-- -->&nbsp;</div><div class=\"ministry-terms-support\"><a id=\"terms-of-service\" href=\"/terms\">Terms and Conditions</a>&nbsp; | &nbsp;<a href=\"https://support.bible.is/contact\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\" id=\"help-support\">Help &amp; Support</a></div></div></section></main>"
